Thank you for joining us for Referenda 2018. Other results will be coming in overnight. We'll have all the referenda results posted on our website tomorrow morning at https://t.co/ENwHkb5bAM.
Congratulations to Winona Area Schools. The district passed a $9.4 million bond for security and renovations by a vote of 8,588 to 6,746.
Rockford Area Schools split referenda votes. A $750 per pupil operating levy passed 2,481 to 2,271. But a $6.8 million technology levy failed by 2,329 to 2,425.
Congratulations to Northfield Public Schools. The district passed a $40.9 million bond for a new elementary, renovations, additions by a vote of 8,874 to 5,382.
Congratulations to Holdingford Public Schools. The district passed an 11.1 million bond for additions, safety, security and maintenance by a vote of 1,419 to 1,031 AND passed a $200 per pupil operating levy 1,235 to 1,216.
Barnesville Public Schools narrowly lost a $26 million bond for renovations and a new high school and elementary by a vote of 1,037 yes to 1,177 no.
Congratulations to Eden Valley-Watkins Public Schools. The district passed a $8 million bond for security, roof, HVAC and ADA compliance by a vote of 1,085 to 965.
Congratulations to St. Paul Public Schools. The district passed a $1,179 per pupil operating levy by a vote of 39,764 to 20,288.
Congratulations to Atwater-Cosmos-Grove City Public Schools. The district passed a $15.5 million bond for maintenance and updates by a vote of 1,266 to 1,244.
Congratulations to Plainview-Elgin-Millville. The district passed a $15.5 million bond for HVAC, security renovations and classroom additions by a vote of 1,891 to 1,299.
Congratulations to Janesville-Waldorf-Pemberton. The district passed an operating levy renewal of $1,610 per pupil by a vote of 1,419 to 756.
Congratulations to Waterville-Elysian-Morristown. The district passed a $19.3 million bond for security, HVAC and maintenance by a vote of 1,955 to 1,154.
Congratulations to Randolph Public Schools. The district passed a $6.8 million bond for renovations and classroom additions by a vote of 761 to 596.
Congratulations to Robbinsdale Public Schools. The district passed a $515 per pupil operating levy 29,166 to 18,242.
Congratulations to Columbia @CHPSisd13 who passed a $12.4 million bond for elementary improvements and safety 6,177 to 4,413 AND passed a 1.75 million bond for high school performing arts center improvements 5,891 to 4,639 AND passed a $2.78 million bond for a band room addition.
RT @Mankatonews: Janesville-Waldorf-Pemberton School District levy renewal referendum passes with 65% in support.
Minneapolis Public Schools passed a $490 per pupil operating levy 148,473 to 42,4009 AND passed a technology capital projects levy by a vote of 123,374 to 52,724. Congratulations!
Congratulations to Edgerton Public Schools. The district passed an operating level renewal of $641 per pupil 814 to 192!
Congratulations to Centennial School District. The district passed a $650 per pupil operating levy 9739 to 6638 AND passed a $22.2 million bond request 9,344 to 6,981.
